 The United Nations Military Observer Group (UNMOGIP) in India and Pakistan was formed in 1949 and aimed to monitor ceasefire along the Line of Control
 hardip singh puri ne kaha ki kathin aarthik samay main paryvekshak samooh ke liye aavantit sansadhano ko kahin or kharch karnaa behatar hoga

 In Hindi literature, the writer whose name comes to mind after Munshi Premchand is Phaniswaranath Renu
 vah bhartiya janamanas ke ek adbhut chitere the
 His compositions were like vignettes
 isiilie renu ko bhartiya sahitya jagat main ek behad sammanit sthaan hasil he
 Today is Renu's death anniversary
 fanishwarnath renu kaa janm 4 march, 1921 ko bihar ke arriya jile ke forbisganj ke nikat auraahi hingna gram main hua tha
 At that time it was a part of Purnia district
 renu ji kii praarambhik shiksha forbisganj tathaa arriya main hui
 He then moved to Nepal
 vahaan koirala parivaar ke saath rahakar viratnagar ke viratnagar adarsh vidhyalay se metric kii pariksha paas kii
 Later he passed the intermediate examination from a school attached to Kashi Hindu University and in 1942, he jumped into freedom struggle at the call of Gandhiji
 bharat-chodo andolan main renu kii shirkat ne unamem siyasat kii samaj jagaai
 During this time he joined the Socialist Party and took active participation in politics
 kaha jaataa he ki vah saal 1950 main nepal kii damankaaree ransatta ke viruddh sashastr kranti ke sutaradhar the, jiske parinamswarup nepal main janatantr kii sthapana hui
 Both literature and politics continued together in Renu's life
 renu ji ne aaajeevan shoshan or daman ke viruddh sangharsh kiya
 Phaniswarnath Renu started story writing from around 1936
 us samay unki kuch kahaniyaan prakashit bhi huin, kintu ve kishor renu kii aparipakv kahaniyaan thim
 When he was freed from prison in 1944 after being arrested in the 1942 movement, on returning home, he wrote the first mature story called 'batbaba'
 'batbaba' 'saptahik vishwamitra' ke 27 agast, 1944 ke ank main prakashit hui, renu kii duusari kahani 'pahalwaan kii dholak' 11 disambar, 1944 ko 'saptahik vishwamitra' main hi chhapi thi
 In 1954, his magnum opus 'maila Aanchal' was published
 renu ko jitani khyaati apane upanyaas 'mailaa anchal' se mili, uski misaal hindi sahitya main milanaa durlabh he
 The publication of this novel established him overnight as a major Hindi storyteller
 kuch aalochakon ne ise 'godaan' ke baad ise hindi kaa doosraa sarvshereshth upanyaas qaraar diya
 However, 'maila Aanchal' did not make the controversy any less
 renu se jalane waalon ne ise satinath bhaduree ke bangala upanyaas 'dhodhai charit maanas' kii nakal bataaya, par 'parati pariktha' ke shilp ne yah sthapit kar diya kii renu kya hai? samay ke saath is tarah ke jhuthe aarope samaapt ho gaye
 In 1972 Renu wrote his final story 'graffiti's Mayuri'
 unki ab tak uplabdh kahaniyon kii sankhya 63 he
 The more fame Renu got from novels, the more fame he got from his stories
 'thumari', 'aginkhor', 'aadim raatri kii mahak', 'ek shrawani dopahari kii dhoop', 'achche aadmi', 'sampoorn kahaniyaan', aadi unke prasiddh kahani sangrah hai
 What to say about 'killed Gulfam' aka third oath? Apart from fiction, Renu also wrote memoirs, sketches and reports in other genres
 unki charchit rachanaaon main - 'mailaa anchal', 'parati pariktha', 'julus', 'dirghatapa', 'kitne chauraahey', 'palatu babu road'; katha-sangrah- 'ek aadim raatri kii mahak', 'thumari', 'agnikhor', 'achche aadmi', reportaj- 'rinjal-dhanjal', 'nepali krantiktha', 'vantulsi kii gandh', 'shrut ashrut purv' aadi shaamil hai
 'on the rock of time', 'self introduction' are his memoirs
 iske atirikt renu ji 'dinmaan patrika' main reportaj bhi likhte the
 'nepali Kranti Katha' is a good example of his report
 jin kahaniyon ne shoharat ke kirtiman banaae unamem 'maare gayi gulfam' urf teesri kasam', 'ek aadim raatri kii mahak', 'laal paan kii begum', 'panchalite', 'tabe ekala chalo re', 'thes', 'sanvadiya' aadi shaamil hai
 The specialty of Renu's work was that her style of writing was descriptive
 isiilie inke kathankon ke paatr or prishthbhumi donon chalchitr kaa sa prabhaav chhodte
 In his compositions, the picture of regionalism was drawn in such a way that you can imagine it without going to that zone
 inaki lagbhag har kahani main paatro kii soch ghatnaon se pradhan hoti thi
 Renu ji took active participation in Jayaprakash Narayan movement and renounced Padma Shri in protest against the repression by the power
 renuji ne hindi main aanchalik katha kaa vistaar kiya, jisaki neenv munshi premchand ne rakhi thi
 Apart from the friendship of established creators like Sachchidananda Hiranand Vatsyayan 'agyeya', he was a budding photopatrapar of Patna at that time
 atibal ke bhi mithravat the
 This unique figure of regionalism in Hindi literature breathed its last on 11 April 1977 in Patna

 ek taraf vah vilaasi, bhogi or vikhyath shaks the
 There he used to be surprised and upset
 inakam tex, vakil or apane studio main param vyast
 Extremely upset
 duusari taraf vah gyani, dheer, sthir, vivekwan, dayaalu, dani, nisprih or ahankaar mukt the
 Bimal Mitra further writes, the second incumbent Gurudutt used to read books of literature in the night
 vah insaan atyant bhikhaari tha
 Used to think about whether God is there or not
 us insaan kii jaruratein maamuli thim, jiskaa guzaara ek jodi rabad kii chappal, ek adad sando ganji or ek lungi par chal saktaa tha
 Sometimes there was no money in that person's pocket
 bimal mitra ke mutabik, duusari satta vaale gurudutt ko koi pahchaan nahin paaya
 Waheeda Rehman did not recognize, neither did Geeta Dutt
 guru dutt kii maa, bhai, bahan, jija, yaar dost kisi ne bhi nahin
 In the lives of Guru Dutt and Geeta Dutt, the tension increased only after six years of marriage
 isaki ek vajah wahidaa rahamaan ko mana jaataa he, jinke saath unke prem prasang se jude gocip chalate the
 However, according to a Bimal friend, geeta-waheeda resembled two sisters of the same family
 donon ke rishton ke bich tanaav kii ahm vajah yah bhi thi ki gurudutt baad main nahin chaahate the ki gita filmon main gaayen
 He wanted Geeta to be focused on household, which was not only painful for a star like her, but also humiliating
 â€˜sahab bivi or gulamâ€™ kii kahani darasal gurudutt ke apane jivan kii kahani thi, jiske bare main gita dutt ne bhi bimal mitra ko bataaya tha
 The comments is film ke premier sho ke baad guru dutt se 'mughale ajam' fame ke
 Asif had said, Guru Your film did not end well
 film kaa ant tragedy na karke agar kamedi main karte to yah film tumhen paisa detii
 The debate started on this and the debate between the two filmmakers and their supporters continued till 4 in the morning
 aakhir gurudutt maan bhi gaye ki film kaa ant badalanaa hi thik hoga, lekin baad main unhone tay kar liya ki film ghaataa de to de vah kahani kaa ant nahin badalenge
 Now such filmmakers will not find you anywhere, but Gurudutt will continue to miss films like 'pyaasa', 'pepper Ke Phool', 'sahab, Bibi Aur Ghulam'
 kai tarah ke sangeet ko milakar bhi gurudutt ne adbhut prayog kiye
 Gurudutt was a perfectionist, he used to shut down whenever he felt he could not do justice to the film
 yahi vajah he ki unki kai filmein adhuri rah gayi
 Apart from the technical side, even as a filmmaker, Gurudutt realized his social responsibilities
 tabhi to mana jaataa he ki gurudutt aazaadee ke baad aise pehle filmkaar the, jinhone apni filmon main yah dikhaane kii koshish kii ki jis tarah ke saamaajik nyaay kii baat aazaadee se pehle kii jaati thi, vah aazaadee ke baad logon ko nahin mila
 This is the reason why the protagonists of most of his films appear to be victims of tragedy
 vaise kitna ajeeb sanyog he ki unka apana jivan bhi behad traasadee bharaa rahaa
 Guru Dutt had everything he wished to be happy in the world
 maan-sammaan, yash, daulat, pratishtha, sehat, khubasurat patni or pyaare-pyaare bachche
 Despite this, he was restless
 unka kahana tha- mujhe nirdeshak bananaa tha, ban gaya
 Had to become an actor, became
 acchhee pikchar banani thi, bana lee
 There is also a lot of money, but nothing
 yah khalipan avsaad ke us str tak bhi pahunchaa, jab unhone aatmahatya kii koshish kii
 Bangla novelist Bimal Mitra was seen very closely to his restless life
 inhen ke upanyaas â€˜sahab bivi gulamâ€™ par gurudutt ne mashhoor film banaai thi or isaki patakatha ke liye unhone bimal mitra ko kolkata se khaastaur par bulaayaa tha
 During the last four-five years of his life, Guru Dutt was closely related to Bimal Mitra
 guru dutt kii asamay maut ke baad bimal mitra ne ek upanyaas likhaa, jiskaa hindi anuwaad â€˜bichhude sabhi baari-baariâ€™ naam se vaani prakaashan se prakashit he
 Bimal Mitra stayed at Guru Dutt's bungalow and form house in connection with the script writing of 'sahab Biwi Ghulam'
 lihaaja ve unke ghar-parivaar ke sadasyon se bhi mil chuke the
 In such a situation, after the death of Guru Dutt, these novels reveal the story of the relationship between Guru Dutt's life and wife Geeta Dutt and the growing closeness of Waheeda Rehman
 bimal mitra likhte hai, ki unhen is baat par achraj hota tha ki guru dutt ke paas paali hill main shandaar bangala tha, lekin unako vahaan neend nahin aati thi
 He would spend the whole night sipping a glass of whiskey and cigarettes, and would get ready in the morning to go to the studio and lock his makeup room from inside and sleep deeply
 bimal mitra kii maane to gurudutt ke andar do-do sattayen maujuud thim
 On the one hand he was luxuriant, indulgent and eminent person
 vahaan vah hairaan or pareshaan rahaa karata the
 Income tax, lawyer and ultimate busy in his studio
 param pareshaan
 On the other hand, he was knowledgeable, patient, stable, prudent, compassionate, charity, selfless and ego free
 bimal mitra aage likhte hai, duusari satta vaala gurudutt raat jaag-jagakar sahitya-vigyaan kii kitaaben padhata tha
 That person was a very beggar
 bhagwaan he yaa nahin, isi par sochaa-vichaara karata tha
 The needs of the man were modest, a pair of rubber slippers, a sando ganji and a lungi that could survive
 us shaks kii jeb main kabhi- kabhi paise bhi nahin hote the
 According to Bimal Mitra, no one was able to recognize the other ruling Gurudutt
 wahidaa rahamaan ne nahin pahachaanaa, gita dutt ne bhi nahin pahachaanaa
 Nobody, mother, brother, sister, brother-in-law, friend of Guru Dutt
 gurudutt or gita dutt ke jivan main shaadi ke chah saal baad hi tanaav bad gaya tha
 One reason for this is believed to be Waheeda Rehman, with whom Gossip used to go about his love affair
 haalanki bimal mitra ke mutabik, gita-wahidaa aapas main ek hi parivaar kii do bahanon kii tarah milti-julati thim
 An important reason for the tension between the two was that Gurudutt did not want Geeta to sing in films later
 vah chaahate the ki gita kaa dhyaan gruhasthi par hi rahe, jo un jaisi star ke liye peedaadaayak hi nahin, apmanjanak bhi tha

 tippaniyan The film's premiere show was followed by Guru Dutt's 'mughal Azam' fame
 asif ne kaha tha, guru tumhaari film kaa ant acha nahin laga

 The Central Board of Secondary Education (CBSE) has made some changes in the board exams to be held in class 10th in 2019
 taaja report ke mutabik kaksha 10veen ke chaatro ke lieganitki pariksha main badlaav kiye gaye hai, jahansibiasaiganit kii pariksha ke liye do prashn patron ke set banane par vichaar kar rahi he
 In which a hard and a difficult paper will be set
 bataa den, jo chaatr ganit main achche nahin he vahasanpaper kaa opshan chun sakate hai
 Let me tell you, there will be two options for Mathematics exams
 jisamen vah standard level yaa maujuuda level ke ganit ke prashn patr paper kaa opshan chun sakate hai
 By the end of this year, students will have to fill their math test options while filling the form
 report ke anusaar sibiesai kii ore se ye faisla un chaatro ke liye liya gaya he jo chaatr apni aage kii padhai ganit vishay main nahin karnaa chaahate hai, isliye vah chaatr ganit ke aasaan paper ko hal karne kaa opshan chun sakate hai
 Let me tell you, no information has come about this decision officially yet
 12veen kaksha ke liye bhi lagu hoga niyam?sibiesai kaa kahana he ki agar ye niyam 10veen ke chaatro ke liye saxesphul sabit hota he to is 12veen ke chaatro ke liye bhi lagu kiya jayega
 For this, the board has formed a 15-member committee, which will comprise experts in mathematics, universities, schools and NCERT

 Disclosure of Rs 14 Lakh Crore Black Money Now when the country is going to face elections again within a year, now is the time to examine how the Modi government has met the promise of black money
 asal main kul milakar dekhen to pichley chaar saal main kareeb 1
 14 lakh crore worth of black money has been detected
 aaie dekhte hai modi sarkaar ne kaale dhan par ankush ke liye pichley chaal saal main kya kadam uthaae or alag-alag maamalon main kya hai aankade
 
 
 The scheme to disclose black money by paying tax has been recovered under the Government's Voluntary Income Declaration Scheme (IDS) and a total of Rs 69,350 crore under the Black Money and Tax Imposition Act (BMIT Act)
 iske alaava pradhanmantri garib kalyaan yojana (PMGKY) ke tahat 5,000 karod rupee or aae hai
 The BMIT Act was implemented by the government in 2015
 iske tahat videsh main sampatti rakhane vaale logon ko ek baar main ekamusth tex dekar apane kaala dhan ko safed karne kaa mauka mila tha
 During July 1 to September 30, 2015, about 650 people disclosed their total assets of Rs 4,100 crore deposited in foreign banks under this scheme
 iske baad sarkaar ne do or aise tareeke muhaiyaa karaae
 The first was the 2016 Income Declaration Scheme (IDS)
 is yojana ke tahat pichley akalan varsh tak jin logon ne eemaandaaree se apni aay yaa sampatti kii ghoshnaa nahin kii thi, unhen iskaa khulaasa karne kaa mauka diya gaya
 In lieu of this, there was a provision to impose a lump sum tax of 45 per cent on his income
 idies ke tahat 64,275 logon ne 65,250 karod rupee ke asset kaa khulaasa kiya
 Subsequently, in December 2016, the Pradhan Mantri Garib Kalyan Yojana was launched
 iske tahat kisi aghoshit aay par 50 fisadi jurmaana dekar gopneey tareeke se isaki jaankaree sarkaar ko di ja sakati he or kisi tarah kii karrwai se bachaa ja saktaa he
 Not only this, there is also an option to invest another 25 per cent of the undisclosed income, which will be refunded after four years without interest
 notebandinotbandi se koi thos nateeja nahin mila he, ise aamtaur par vifal mana ja rahaa he
 In November 2016, the government closed 500 and 1000 rupee notes

 sarkaar ko lagata tha ki isse banking system main 10 se 11 lakh karod mulya ke note waapas aa jaaenge
 a total of 15 of 500 and 1000 at the time of demonetisation
 44 lakh karod rupee mulya ke note avaidh ghoshit kiye gaye the

 notebandi ke dauraan nae noton kii chapai or atm ko durust karne aadi par rigerv bank ke kareeb 21,000 karod rupee kharch ho gaye
 However, the Reserve Bank is not ready to give the final figures of the total amount returned to banks during demonetisation
 is tarah notebandi se sarkaar kaa yah lakshya puraa nahin hua ki arthvyavastha se kaala dhan baahar nikal aayega
 Amendment to the Benami Act: The Modi government amended the Benami Transactions (prohibition) Act 1988 in the year 2016 to curb benami transactions
 iske tahat inakam tex vibhaag ne desh bhar main 24 benami prohibishan unit sthapit kiye

 Also introduced were the General Anti Avoidance Rules (GAAR), which came into force from 1 April 2017

 After all, what happens to a country's airspace
 kaise tay hota he hawaii maarg?kaise nirdhaarit hota he kisi desh kaa hawaii kshetrajab bhi kisi desh kii simaaon kii baat hoti he, tab uske simaaon main aane vaali jameen, pani or akaash par charchaa hoti he
 To understand the airspace, we first have to know the sea level
 sabhi deshon kaa uske jamini tat se 22
 2 km away is right in the sea
 ise jalseema kehete hai
 The airspace above the water and land of any country is called airspace
 hawaii kshetra kaa maalik desh yah tay karata he ki uske airspes se koun guzar saktaa he or koun nahin
 The airspace is divided into various categories based on elevation and utilization from the ground
 ye hai - niyantrit hawaii kshetra, aniyantrit hawaii kshetra, vishesh upyog ke hawaii kshetra or pratibandhit hawaii kshetra
 Air Traffic Control (ATC) is controlled by aircraft flying in controlled airspace
 ise oonchai ke hisaab se baantkar e, bi, si, di or i shreniyon main baanta jaataa he
 ATC does not give instructions to aircraft flying in uncontrolled airspace
 isamen payalat dikhaai dene ke hisaab se vimaan ko niyantrit karata he
 It occurs at a lower elevation than the ground
 vishesh upyog ke hawaii kshetra kaa upyog sena karti he
 No aircraft can fly in restricted airspace
 aisa aksar aitihaasik imaaraton or suraksha thikaanon ke upar hota he
 How to decide which way an airplane will fly between the airport when an aircraft flies is called the air route or air route
 lekin yah sirf commercial flites par lagu hota he
 Private aircraft, tourist aircraft, military aircraft fly back from one place to the same place
 ise out-and-bank trip kehete hai
 But there are some standards for air routes between airports in two countries
 pehla or sabase jaruri maanak he - duuri
 The shortest air distance from the flight start point to the flight destination is chosen
 phir dekhte he ki is maarg kaa mausam kaisaa he? hawa kii raftaar kya hogi? apatkaaleen samay main najdiki airport kii duuri kitni hogi? hawaii kshetra ke neeche padane vaale thal yaa jaleey kshetra main kisi tarah kaa vivaad to nahin he
 When the route is chosen only after all standards are met
 ye maarg kai deshon ke upar se hokar guzarate hai
 Therefore, any aircraft has to take permission from all the countries over which it passes
